type="application/ld+json">{"@context":{"@vocab":"http://schema.org","articleId":{"@id":"Text","@type":"@id"},"topics":{"@id":"Text","@type":"@id"}},"@type":"NewsArticle","headline":"RFK Jr. says he is being investigated for collecting whale specimen","url":"https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/rfk-jr-says-investigated-collecting-whale-specimen-rcna171178","thumbnailUrl":"https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_social_share_1024x768_scale,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg","alternativeHeadline":"RFK Jr. says he is being investigated for collecting whale specimen","articleBody":"GLENDALE, Ariz. — Former independent presidential candidate Robert F. Kennedy Jr. said Saturday he is being investigated for collecting a whale specimen. \"I received a letter from the National Marine Fisheries Institute saying that they were investigating me for collecting a whale specimen 20 years ago,\" Kennedy said during a campaign event for former President Donald Trump in Glendale, Arizona, noting that he received the letter \"this week.\" Kennedy said that he responded in a letter, baselessly linking the National Marine Fisheries Service with whale deaths and calling for the agency to investigate.   \"This is all about the weaponization of our government against political opponents,\" he said. Kennedy did not go into details about the whale incident, but his daughter had previously described a situation involving a whale that took place 30 years ago. His daughter Kathleen \"Kick\" Kennedy, 36, described in a 2012 article for Town & Country magazine how, when she was 6, her father used a chainsaw to cut the head off a dead whale that had washed ashore and bungee-corded it to the family's car during their drive home.  \"Every time we accelerated on the highway, whale juice would pour into the windows of the car, and it was the rankest thing on the planet,\" she told the magazine at the time. \"We all had plastic bags over our heads with mouth holes cut out, and people on the highway were giving us the finger, but that was just normal day-to-day stuff for us.\" Robert F. Kennedy Jr.'s comments came during a campaign event alongside former Hawaii Rep. Tulsi Gabbard for Trump at Arizona Christian University. Kennedy endorsed Trump in August and has since been on the campaign trail urging supporters to back the former president. Kennedy told NBC News after the program that he has never killed a whale.  The National Marine Fisheries Service, which is part of the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration, did not immediately respond to a request for comment and confirmation Saturday night.  When asked by a reporter after the campaign event for details about the investigation, Kennedy said he was \"not going to talk\" about the incident, but would talk about \"serious policy issues.\" He criticized the media as wanting to discuss \"gossipy nonsense,\" adding, \"I’m not interested in feeding that feature of mainstream media.\" After the 2012 story resurfaced last month, an environmental group urged federal officials to investigate the incident.  \"Kennedy may think that his name and privilege mean the rules don’t apply to him, but if he had a shred of integrity left he’d surrender this whale skull and any other illegally collected wildlife parts to the authorities,\" said Brett Hartl, political director for the Center for Biological Diversity Action Fund, in a news release. \"If he doesn’t, NOAA law enforcement should open an investigation and potentially bring charges against him.\" Kennedy previously faced blowback for saying in August that he had once put a young dead bear in Central Park after planning to skin the bear for meat. He described in a video ultimately deciding to try to make it look like the cub got hit by a bike in the park, saying, \"We thought it would be amusing for whoever found it.\" The New York State Department of Environmental Conservation said at the time it is against the law to dispose of a dead bear in the way Kennedy said he did. The statute of limitations for such offenses, which are subject to a fine, is a year, it said.  Alex Tabet reported from Glendale, Arizona, and Megan Lebowitz from Washington, D.C.","dateCreated":"2024-09-15T03:50:35.000Z","datePublished":"2024-09-15T03:50:35.000Z","dateModified":"2024-09-15T03:50:35.000Z","articleSection":"politics","articleId":"rcna171178","identifier":{"@type":"PropertyValue","propertyID":"uid","value":"rcna171178"},"topics":"","image":{"@type":"ImageObject","url":"https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-1500w,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg","caption":"Former Independent candidate for president Robert F. Kennedy Jr., left, speaks as former Democratic Rep. Tulsi Gabbard listens at a campaign event for former President Donald Trump, Saturday, Sept. 14, 2024, in Glendale, Ariz. class="article-body layout-grid-item layout-grid-item--with-gutter-s-only grid-col-10-m grid-col-push-1-m grid-col-6-xl grid-col-push-2-xl article-body--custom-column"><section class="mb7"><div target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="styles_link__RsJVU"><span class="icon icon-share-facebook"></span></a></li><li data-testid="social-share-twitter" class="styles_item__b5A78 styles_twitter__ww7sF"><a class="styles_button__b3sx_"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></button><div class="styles_copyTooltip__Ut_t1"><span class="icon icon-alt-check"></span></div></li><li data-testid="social-share-sms" class="styles_item__b5A78 styles_sms__Vohh6"><a href="sms:?&amp;body=RFK Jr. says he is being investigated for collecting whale specimen via nbcnews - https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/rfk-jr-says-investigated-collecting-whale-specimen-rcna171178" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="styles_link__RsJVU"><span class="icon icon-sms"></span></a></li><li data-testid="social-share-save" class="styles_save__ILVuj"></li></ul></div><div class="article-body__date-source" data-testid="article-body-timestamp"><time class="relative z-1" dateTime="2024-09-15T03:50:35.854Z" data-testid="timestamp__datePublished" content="2024-09-15T03:50:35.854Z">Sept. 15, 2024, 3:50 AM UTC</time></div><div class="article-inline-byline" data-activity-map="inline-byline-article-top">By <span class="byline-name" data-testid="byline-name"><a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/author/alex-tabet-ncpn1237627">Alex Tabet</a></span> and <span class="byline-name" data-testid="byline-name"><a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/author/megan-lebowitz-ncpn1275337">Megan Lebowitz</a></span></div></section><div class="article-body__content"><p class="">GLENDALE, Ariz. — Former independent presidential candidate <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/rfk-jr-will-appear-michigan-ballot-state-supreme-court-rules-rcna170289" target="_blank">Robert F. Kennedy Jr. </a>said Saturday he is being investigated for collecting a whale specimen.</p><p class=""><em>"</em>I received a letter from the National Marine Fisheries Institute saying that they were investigating me for collecting a whale specimen 20 years ago," Kennedy said during a campaign event for former President Donald Trump in Glendale, Arizona, noting that he received the letter "this week."</p><div class="ad ad--text-alignment ad-container boxinlineAd dn-print" data-testid="ad__container"><div data-mps="true" data-slot="boxinline" data-sizes="[[[1000,1],[]],[[758,1],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[728,90],[360,360]]],[[0,0],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[360,360]]]]" data-render-on-view="true" data-targeting="{}" data-active-tab="true" data-offset-viewport="100" data-testid="ad__container__inner"></div></div><div id="taboolaReadMoreBelow"></div><p class="">Kennedy said that he responded in a letter, baselessly linking the National Marine Fisheries Service with whale deaths and calling for the agency to investigate.  </p><figure class="styles_inlineImage__yAWZ0 styles_medium__OMa6x"><picture class="styles_image__1qciH" data-testid="picture"><source media="(min-width: 1000px)" srcSet="https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-560w,f_avif,q_auto:eco,dpr_2/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg 2x, https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-560w,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg 1x"/><source media="(min-width: 320px)" srcSet="https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-760w,f_avif,q_auto:eco,dpr_2/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg 2x, https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-760w,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg 1x"/><img loading="lazy" src="https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_fit-760w,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-09/240914-rfk-jr-arizona-cc-1105p-d6213b.jpg" alt="Robert F. Kennedy Jr. speaks at a campaign event for former President Donald Trump." height="1667" width="2500"/></picture><figcaption class="caption styles_caption__Pe5JC" data-testid="caption"><span class="caption__container" data-testid="caption__container">Former Independent candidate for president Robert F. Kennedy Jr., left, speaks as former Democratic Rep. Tulsi Gabbard listens at a campaign event for former President Donald Trump, Saturday, Sept. 14, 2024, in Glendale, Ariz. </span><span class="caption__source" data-testid="caption__source">Ross D. Franklin / AP</span></figcaption></figure><p class="">"This is all about the weaponization of our government against political opponents," he said.</p><p class="">Kennedy did not go into details about the whale incident, but his daughter had previously described a situation involving a whale that took place 30 years ago.</p><p class="">His daughter Kathleen "Kick" Kennedy, 36, described in a 2012 article for <a href="https://www.townandcountrymag.com/society/tradition/a924/kick-kennedy-interview/" target="_blank">Town & Country magazine</a> how, when she was 6, her father used a chainsaw to cut the head off a dead whale that had washed ashore and bungee-corded it to the family's car during their drive home. </p><div class="recommended-intersection-ref" data-activity-map="recommended-article-body-recommended" data-testid="recommended-wrapper"></div><div class="recommended-intersection-ref" data-activity-map="recommended-article-body-recommended" data-testid="recommended-wrapper"></div><div class="ad ad--text-alignment ad-container boxinlineAd dn-print" data-testid="ad__container"><div data-mps="true" data-slot="boxinline" data-sizes="[[[1000,1],[]],[[758,1],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[728,90],[360,360]]],[[0,0],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[360,360]]]]" data-render-on-view="true" data-targeting="{}" data-active-tab="true" data-offset-viewport="100" data-testid="ad__container__inner"></div></div><p class="">"Every time we accelerated on the highway, whale juice would pour into the windows of the car, and it was the rankest thing on the planet," she told the magazine at the time. "We all had plastic bags over our heads with mouth holes cut out, and people on the highway were giving us the finger, but that was just normal day-to-day stuff for us."</p><p class="">Robert F. Kennedy Jr.'s comments came during a campaign event alongside former Hawaii Rep. <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/tulsi-gabbard-big-moment-kamala-harris-tuesday-debate-rcna169234" target="_blank">Tulsi Gabbard</a> for Trump at Arizona Christian University. Kennedy <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/rfk-jr-says-court-filing-endorsing-trump-ending-presidential-hopes-rcna165936" target="_blank">endorsed Trump</a> in August and has since been on the campaign trail urging supporters to back the former president.</p><p class="">Kennedy told NBC News after the program that he has never killed a whale. </p><p class="">The National Marine Fisheries Service, which is part of the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration, did not immediately respond to a request for comment and confirmation Saturday night. </p><p class="">When asked by a reporter after the campaign event for details about the investigation, Kennedy said he was "not going to talk" about the incident, but would talk about "serious policy issues." He criticized the media as wanting to discuss "gossipy nonsense," adding, "I’m not interested in feeding that feature of mainstream media."</p><p class="">After the 2012 story resurfaced last month, an environmental group urged federal officials to investigate the incident. </p><div class="ad ad--text-alignment ad-container boxinlineAd dn-print" data-testid="ad__container"><div data-mps="true" data-slot="boxinline" data-sizes="[[[1000,1],[]],[[758,1],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[728,90],[360,360]]],[[0,0],[[300,250],[700,50],[5,5],[360,360]]]]" data-render-on-view="true" data-targeting="{}" data-active-tab="true" data-offset-viewport="100" data-testid="ad__container__inner"></div></div><p class="">"Kennedy may think that his name and privilege mean the rules don’t apply to him, but if he had a shred of integrity left he’d surrender this whale skull and any other illegally collected wildlife parts to the authorities," said Brett Hartl, political director for the Center for Biological Diversity Action Fund, in a <a href="https://centeractionfund.org/federal-officials-urged-to-investigate-kennedys-unlawful-scavenging-of-dead-whale/" target="_blank">news</a><a href="https://centeractionfund.org/federal-officials-urged-to-investigate-kennedys-unlawful-scavenging-of-dead-whale/" target="_blank"> </a><a href="https://centeractionfund.org/federal-officials-urged-to-investigate-kennedys-unlawful-scavenging-of-dead-whale/" target="_blank">re</a><a href="https://centeractionfund.org/federal-officials-urged-to-investigate-kennedys-unlawful-scavenging-of-dead-whale/" target="_blank">lease.</a> "If he doesn’t, NOAA law enforcement should open an investigation and potentially bring charges against him."</p><p class="">Kennedy previously <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/robert-f-kennedy-jr-posts-video-saying-put-young-dead-bear-central-par-rcna165095" target="_blank">faced blowback</a> for saying in August that he had once put a young dead bear in Central Park after planning to skin the bear for meat. He described in a video ultimately deciding to try to make it look like the cub got hit by a bike in the park, saying, "We thought it would be amusing for whoever found it."</p><p class="">The New York State Department of Environmental Conservation said at the time it is <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2024-election/rfk-jr-faced-fine-dumping-dead-bear-central-park-rcna165275" target="_blank">against the law to dispose of a dead bear</a> in the way Kennedy said he did. The statute of limitations for such offenses, which are subject to a fine, is a year, it said. </p><p class="endmark"><em>Alex Tabet reported from Glendale, Arizona, and Megan Lebowitz from Washington, D.C.</em></p></div><div class="article-body__content"><div class="expanded-byline-contributors articleBylineContainer"><div class="expanded-byline article-expanded-byline" of his daughters, Kathleen “Kick” Kennedy, described in a 2012 article how her father cut the head off a dead whale that had washed ashore and bungee-corded it to the family’s car.","content":{"text":["GLENDALE, Ariz. — Former independent presidential candidate Robert F. Kennedy Jr. said Saturday he is being investigated for collecting a whale specimen.","\"I received a letter from the National Marine Fisheries Institute saying that they were investigating me for collecting a whale specimen 20 years ago,\" Kennedy said during a campaign event for former President Donald Trump in Glendale, Arizona, noting that he received the letter \"this week.\"","Kennedy said that he responded in a letter, baselessly linking the National Marine Fisheries Service with whale deaths and calling for the agency to investigate.  ","\"This is all about the weaponization of our government against political opponents,\" he said.","Kennedy did not go into details about the whale incident, but his daughter had previously described a situation involving a whale that took place 30 years ago.","His daughter Kathleen \"Kick\" Kennedy, 36, described in a 2012 article for Town \u0026 Country magazine how, when she was 6, her father used a chainsaw to cut the head off a dead whale that had washed ashore and bungee-corded it to the family's car during their drive home. ","\"Every time we accelerated on the highway, whale juice would pour into the windows of the car, and it was the rankest thing on the planet,\" she told the magazine at the time. \"We all had plastic bags over our heads with mouth holes cut out, and people on the highway were giving us the finger, but that was just normal day-to-day stuff for us.\"","Robert F. Kennedy Jr.'s comments came during a campaign event alongside former Hawaii Rep. Tulsi Gabbard for Trump at Arizona Christian University. Kennedy endorsed Trump in August and has since been on the campaign trail urging supporters to back the former president.","Kennedy told NBC News after the program that he has never killed a whale. ","The National Marine Fisheries Service, which is part of the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration, did not immediately respond to a request for comment and confirmation Saturday night. ","When asked by a reporter after the campaign event for details about the investigation, Kennedy said he was \"not going to talk\" about the incident, but would talk about \"serious policy issues.\" He criticized the media as wanting to discuss \"gossipy nonsense,\" adding, \"I’m not interested in feeding that feature of mainstream media.\"","After the 2012 story resurfaced last month, an environmental group urged federal officials to investigate the incident. ","\"Kennedy may think that his name and privilege mean the rules don’t apply to him, but if he had a shred of integrity left he’d surrender this whale skull and any other illegally collected wildlife parts to the authorities,\" said Brett Hartl, political director for the Center for Biological Diversity Action Fund, in a news release. \"If he doesn’t, NOAA law enforcement should open an investigation and potentially bring charges against him.\"","Kennedy previously faced blowback for saying in August that he had once put a young dead bear in Central Park after planning to skin the bear for meat. He described in a video ultimately deciding to try to make it look like the cub got hit by a bike in the park, saying, \"We thought it would be amusing for whoever found it.\"","The New York State Department of Environmental Conservation said at the time it is against the law to dispose of a dead bear in the way Kennedy said he did. The statute of limitations for such offenses, which are subject to a fine, is a year, it said. ","Alex Tabet reported from Glendale, Arizona, and Megan Lebowitz from Washington, D.C."]},"documentTracing":{"currentMessageId":{"id":"66b9903f-cdcf-4706-a0f6-2f7e24833eab","updatedDate":"Sun Sep 15 2024 15:52:30 GMT+0000
